                                        <h2 class="title">Best and Worst</h2>
                                        <div class="newsContainer">
                                            
                                                <div class="newsContainerItem" data-qa="best-worst-item">
                                                    <a href="https://editorial.rottentomatoes.com/article/sidney-poitiers-7-most-memorable-performances/" class="articleLink unstyled" data-qa="best-worst-link">
                                                        <div class="newsPhoto js-lazyLoad" data-src="https://s3-us-west-2.amazonaws.com/flx-editorial-wordpress/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/09155023/Sidney-Poitier-Memorable.jpg" data-bg-image="true"></div>

    <aside id="interscroller_ad" class="interscroller_ad visible-xs center mobile-interscroller " style="width:300px"></aside>
    <script>
        var mps = mps || {};
        mps._queue = mps._queue || {};
        mps._queue.gptloaded = mps._queue.gptloaded || [];
        mps._queue.adload = mps._queue.adload || [];

        mps._queue.gptloaded.push(function() {
            if (mps.getResponsiveSet() =='0') { //MOBILE
                mps.insertAd('#interscroller_ad','interscroller');
            }
        });
        mps._queue.adload.push(function(eo) {
            if (eo._mps._slot === 'interscroller' && eo.isEmpty) {
                document.querySelector('.mobile-interscroller').classList.add('isEmpty');
            }
        });
    </script>

    <h2 class="panel-heading" data-qa="videos-section-title">
        
            <em>Klaus</em>

<section id="audience_reviews" class="panel panel-rt panel-box" data-qa="audience-reviews">
    <h2 class="panel-heading">Audience Reviews for <em>Klaus</em></h2>
    
        
        <div class="sr-only js-clamp-live-region" aria-live="polite"></div>
        <ul class="mop-audience-reviews__reviews-wrap clearfix">
            
            
            
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-left cl" data-qa="quote-bubble">
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">Jan 10, 2021</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">A great retelling of the myth of Santa Claus, this one is just a little bit darker. Still absolutely a kids movie, this one tackles the topics of depression and hope, looking at Santa before he was as jolly as he is these days.</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-wrap">
                        
                            <a href="/user/id/817734815">
                            
                                <img class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-avatar" src="https://graph.facebook.com/v3.3/695372463/picture"></span>
                            
                            </a>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name-wrap">
                            
                                <a href="/user/id/817734815">
                                    <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name">Mark C</span>
                                </a>
                            
                            
                                <strong class="super-reviewer-badge">Super Reviewer</strong>
                            
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </li>
                
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-right cr" data-qa="quote-bubble">
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__half "></span><span class="star-display__empty"></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">Mar 23, 2020</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">Nice animated feature about the origins of Santa Claus, given warmth by the cast, sure, but the script is a touch on the weak side. The kiddies won&#39;t notice, but the parents of said kiddies will find something lacking. For instance, the ship owner is given note for the whole feature, but there&#39;s really no payoff for said character (however nicely realised by Norm MacDonald). Still, a worthy Christmas entree.</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-wrap">
                        
                            <a href="/user/id/787154086">
                            
                                <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-default"></span>
                            
                            </a>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name-wrap">
                            
                                <a href="/user/id/787154086">
                                    <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name">Kevin M. W</span>
                                </a>
                            
                            
                                <strong class="super-reviewer-badge">Super Reviewer</strong>
                            
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </li>
                
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-left cl" data-qa="quote-bubble">
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__half "></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">Dec 31, 2019</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">It&#39;s hard to give to much of a review of this one, it&#39;s just an aggressively likable Christmas movie.  Telling a bit of an origin story to the mythos of Santa Claus through the eyes of a mailman, it&#39;s a movie that&#39;s at times very funny but usually just incredible charming.  If it has a choice between a charming character moment or a big laugh, it&#39;ll go for the charm, and that&#39;s okay.  It makes a very sweet movie that never feels saccharine, but just right.  Oh and did I mention it&#39;s beautiful?  Because holy crap this animation is gorgeous.  If I had a complaint it&#39;d be that there&#39;s a couple pop song moments that don&#39;t quite fit in which almost feels inescapable in an animated film these days, but the biggest thing is that in the third act we get one of those &quot;liar revealed&quot; tropes.  It&#39;s an annoying trope and I hate it, but fortunately it doesn&#39;t last very long and admittedly it does propel the film towards its final message which is a good one.  Other than that, I think we could have a Christmas classic on our hands here.</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-wrap">
                        
                            <a href="/user/id/901376268">
                            
                                <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-default"></span>
                            
                            </a>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name-wrap">
                            
                                <a href="/user/id/901376268">
                                    <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name">Michael M</span>
                                </a>
                            
                            
                                <strong class="super-reviewer-badge">Super Reviewer</strong>
                            
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </li>
                
        </ul>
        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__view-all clearfix">
            <a href="/m/klaus/reviews?type=user" class="mop-audience-reviews__view-all--link" data-qa="audience-reviews-view-all-link">
                See all Audience reviews
            </a>
        </div>
    
</section>
